[30;1m96 | [0m[35mWhen accessing a value or a slice of data in a channel, npTDMS will read whole chunks at a time.[0m

[30;1m98 | [0m[35m:py:meth:`nptdms.TdmsFile.data_chunks`. This is a generator that produces instances of[0m
[30;1m99 | [0m[35m:py:class:`~nptdms.DataChunk`.[0m
